< text>
The customer service and accountability of this store is greatly lacking. Horrible experience. Atrocious staff experience. The store manager double charged me for a purchase and even after I showed him that the transaction went through he said I would need to pay again because he believed it error-ed out.

He then called me back and promised that I would not be doubled charged. Low and behold I got double charged. After calling the store back and speaking with Shannon, who was also little help, told me there is nothing we can do about this in the store and you will need to call customer service. After asking for the number she said she would need to place me on hold in order to find the number, she then left me on hold for 6 minutes. I hung up and then called back just to have her promptly answer the phone and tell me that she was busy with other customers in the store and that is why she left me on hold. After finally getting the Customer service number, I once again had to wait on hold for 22 minutes and then wait for 20 mins just for the customer service department to locate the transaction even after giving them the store code 00746 Transaction # 55 and Hour and Minute of purchase. She then informed me that it would take 10 days for the refund to go through.

So because of the store managers mistake I know have to wait for a refund to be issued on a transaction that was confirmed by the CSR to be a duplicate. I asked to speak with her Manager Gema (Employee # C103193) out of the Mexico call center, based on this experience so far its no surprise that GameStop outsources its customer service teams. Gema barely apologized, it was one of those "Sorry that you have had a bad experience" and that was it, it basically sounded like she was reading off of a script. She told me there was nothing that she could do and they do not provide anything except and apology when the make a mistake. Not a company looking to maintain customers on my opinion. < review>
Leanns nails is a gem of Alameda!! It is one of the only nail spas under the ‚Äú Healthy nail salon program‚Äù so it is incredibly clean and sterile. I am so particular about nail salons bc of all of the fungal horror stories from unclean pedicure tubs (there is no real way to thoroughly sterilize these). Leanne uses a tub covered in a plastic bag where the contents are discarded so no one can use the same bath twice. Obviously, these best practices have adapted for covid standards with dividers between stations, hand sanitizer upon entry, and services appointment only (she does brows too!).

Additionally, Leanne has the sweetest, calm, and beautiful  personality. She is so attentive to the customer needs and preferences -truly goes above and beyond to make sure you are comfortable and satisfied before you leave. Finally, she has been at her location for 25 years so she is dedicated to the craft and you are supporting a small and local East bay lady!<//review>

I am leaving a review not for their service but for a personal experience i encountered from one of  their kind and honest employee. Coming down from Lytle Creek me and my husband decided to stop by the nearest McDonalds to eat and use the restroom. I placed my wallet in my shallow jacket pocket (which was a bad idea) thinking that it would be safe there  as long as my hand is in there holding it. I got so distracted and was overly happy talking to my husband about my first time exprience being in the snow that i  removed my hand from my pocket and stopped holding my wallet (again clumsy me thinking it would be safe there) the moment i stepped in the restroom was then i realized my wallet is no longer in the my pocket.Thinking it fell, I went searching for it all over the gas station retracing my steps but couldn't find it. My name and phone number was pasted in there, so i thought any honest man who picked it up would for sure give me a call. Hours later i received a  call from Ruben, which was one of their employees telling me that he found my wallet. Thank God for honest people. Ruben even gave us a tip not to go  to the high dessert at night since the traffic was so bad. I met the kind Ruben the day after, i am glad he did made sure i was the owner by asking questions through the info from my ID. I could never thank Ruben enough for saving me from requesting new i.d's and for being an honest and kind man. May God bless you. Aguiar's towing is very lucky to have a kind and honest employee. <review>We love Reptacular Ranch! The moment we did our first site visit of the venue we knew it was our wedding venue. Diana was so helpful every time we stopped by to plan things here and there. Cory was always open to quick communication and answering any questions we had. He also put our minds at ease if we had any concerns about anything - and I mean ANYTHING.

The day of it ended up being a little cloudy with some drizzle, but the Ranch still looked beautiful! We utilized the full space, adding some animal experiences along with the petting zoo and our guests loved that there was so much to do during cocktail hour.

This place is a hidden gem and we would choose it all over again in a heartbeat. Thank you to the entire Reptacular Ranch team for making our wedding day so very special!</review>< Pictures>

< review>
My son's wedding was held on 6/22/18. The ceremony was at 5:30 and the party went on until very late into the night.
Ranch staff is amazing!! I can't say enough about how accommodating they were to us prior to the wedding and the day of.

Food: A fun food truck or trucks would be ideal. The ranch currently does not have anywhere to cook or prepare foods. Caterers hired must have outdoor kitchen that they bring with them and they should be highly experienced in outdoor cooking with no sink, cooking source or refrigeration. This is very important for you to note and find solutions to safe eating for your guests. I wish I could have convinced my son to do this but they were set to go with a caterer who did not have this experience.

Venue:  it's simply beautiful. Very rustic and open. The lighting at night is very nice and the tree's light up, its magical.
The owners just added a vineyard. I was disappointed that nothing was growing on it yet, but in a few months it is going to be amazing. They seem to be constantly working on improvements. They planted flower boxes going down the bride path and it would have been nice if they planted white flowers or lavender would be best so it ties with most weddings.
The seat area where guest sit need sails or something to shade guest. They set up four umbrellas and guest tried squeezing under them. I recommend bride party purchase nice shade umbrellas for all guests until this is resolved or trees grow.

Weather: it gets hot, it was 90 degrees and I was very concerned about the flowers. Florist need to know that the flowers of set up to early, will be in full sun.
It starts to cool down in the evening and you will need a light sweater. My son rented 6 heaters which I felt were unnecessary. They were not used and it was a waste of money. There is also a firepit and lots of folks hung out there and made smores.
Do not drink and drive! We provided uber rides to guests and a couple took advantage of it.

Overall it was beautiful.<//review>

< rating>
5</rating>
< text>
Our all time favorite pastry shop in LA since it opened about 13 years ago. Consistent quality and taste. I fell in love with Chantilly when I tasted the fruit tart and strawberry shortcake 12 years ago.  The strawberry slices on top of the cake and between the layers are always fresh (whereas other shops' are overripe or spoiled, even in high end restaurants).  The whip cream and custard used in the cakes were always fresh, light and not too sweet, just enough to highlight the freshness of the key ingredients. Their cream puffs (Sesame cream) are the excellent. Make sure you try the seasonal cakes. Kids who don't like grapefruit will love the grapefruit jelly offered only in summer.<//text>

Certainly a place worth visiting, the food is awesome and well prepared, the prices are reasonable and it is consistently neat in here. Keep it up.<//Text>
<pics>None< /pics><Resp>None< /Resp><gmap_id>0x809ae0c3420f8367:0x34296af27bda3b04</gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
<UserId.>105792666128833345031< /UserId.>< text>
This was my first time at the restaurant and I was excited to try it. My group was excited about the 50% off section. The restaurant is in a funky shopping center near a Nepalese restaurant, taco bell, grocery outlets, and Ross. The overall decor of the restaurant was nice. They have a veggie roll section which i was excited about. A tad disappointed that they couldn't have any veggie rolls in the 50% off rolls. Order 3 rolls and a sake bomb. I was never brought the sake bomb. They did give us some edamame before our food came. After our rolls came out dinner rush just started and we were a little ignored other than for water refills. Additionally, it took awhile to receive our bill, a to go box, and our bills to be processed.

Overall, good sushi but lacking in the service area.<//text>

<gmapID>0x809ae0c3420f8367:0x34296af27bda3b04<//gmapID><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< text>
This small, almost a hole-in-the-wall looking sushi place is really a ("state of the art") modern Sushi House! With indoor waterfall/pond, Sports bar, and modern Japanese wood-works throughout the restaurant. All sushi rolls are 50% off ALWAYS. The menu, however, has a good selection of other Japanese Cuisine choices including vegetarian and vegan. Beer and cocktail selections are limited but good nonetheless.
Every time l had stoped by Blue Nami, lunch or dinner, there is a wait time. This is not always a bad thing, it tells you others are willing to wait for the Blue Nami experience. As am I.< /text>

Have been a returning customer for over a year. The food is good, not the best sushi but is "50%" off and better than all you can eat quality..

<review>It's almost too nice inside. I can't help but wonder how much markup they have lol. That being said I order exclusively on the 50% off menu and its quite good

Update 10/28:
Just grabbed some takeout from here and really felt like I needed to take a star back. They currently have a hostess seating people and also selling takeout orders, which results in a very long wait for those who called ahead. As if the long wait wasn't enough, they do not keep change in their register, because apparently some cashier got change scammed. Lol? You'll have to wait for them to go find an approved staff member to make change.

Maybe train your staff better instead of punishing honest paying customers..

Update 12/8: I've been back since and the food and service was back up to par. Seems like my last visit was a one off thing which is good.

Tried to make a reservation for my birthday tonight and they said they don't take resevations. That's fine. But when I asked how early I should come to put my name in in order to secure a table for 13 she said 20 minutes. Again, that's fine. But, then she said they couldn't take my name unless over half the party was there that ticked me off. I then said "Ok, I guess I will have my birthday dinner somewhere else." The girl said "Ok, that's a good thing." I was baffled. Up until my last statement I was super sweet and she came off rude and unaccomodating. It's unfortunate because we used to eat here a lot. We won't be coming back. I called and made a reservation with Mikuni who gladly took our reservation very last minute. So basically. Do not come here if you have a big party.</review>
